2025-06-01T02:13:01.1058863Z         you can try to use `exclude_package_data`, or `include-package-data=False` in
2025-06-01T02:13:01.1059138Z         combination with a more fine grained `package-data` configuration.
2025-06-01T02:13:01.1059146Z 
2025-06-01T02:13:01.1059438Z         You can read more about "package data files" on setuptools documentation page:
2025-06-01T02:13:01.1059444Z 
2025-06-01T02:13:01.1059770Z         - https://setuptools.pypa.io/en/latest/userguide/datafiles.html
2025-06-01T02:13:01.1059776Z 
2025-06-01T02:13:01.1059780Z 
2025-06-01T02:13:01.1059939Z         [^1]: For Python, any directory (with suitable naming) can be imported,
2025-06-01T02:13:01.1060052Z               even if it does not contain any `.py` files.
2025-06-01T02:13:01.1060218Z               On the other hand, currently there is no concept of package data
2025-06-01T02:13:01.1060446Z               directory, all directories are treated like packages.
